<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>

<td>20 songs
<ol><li> Das Wandern / <i>To Wander</i> (B-flat major)
</li><li> Wohin / <i>Whither</i> (G major)
</li><li> Halt? / <i>Stay?</i> (C major)
</li><li> Danksagung an den Bach / <i>Thanks to the Brook</i> (G major)
</li><li> Am Feierabend / <i>The Hour of Rest</i> (A minor)
</li><li> Der Neugierige / <i>The Eager Questioner</i> (B major)
</li><li> Ungeduld / <i>Impatience</i> (A major)
</li><li> Morgengruss / <i>Good Morning</i> (C major)
</li><li> Des Müllers Blumen / <i>The Miller's Flowers</i> (A major)
</li><li> Tränenregen / <i>Shower of Tears</i> (A major)
</li><li> Mein / <i>Mine</i> (D major)
</li><li> Pause / <i>Interlude</i> (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> major)
</li><li> Mit dem grünen Lautenband / <i>With the Green Lute-riband</i> (B-flat major)
</li><li> Der Jäger / <i>The Hunter</i> (C minor)
</li><li> Eifersucht und Stolz / <i>Jealousy and Pride</i> (G minor)
</li><li> Die liebe Farbe / <i>The Favorite Color</i> (B minor)
</li><li> Die böse Farbe / <i>The Hated Color</i> (B major)
</li><li> Trockne Blumen / <i>Withered Flowers</i> (E minor)
</li><li> Der Müller und der Bach / <i>The Miller and the Brook</i> (G minor)
</li><li> Des Baches Wiegenlied / <i>The Brook's Lullaby</i> (E major)
</li></ol>
